### [217] [Not Every Rubric Teaches Equally: Policy-Aware Rubric Rewards for RLVR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.20164)
*Utkarsh Tyagi,Xingang Guo,MohammadHossein Rezaei,Daniel George,Anas Mahmoud,Jackson Lee,Bing Liu,Yunzhong He*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: POW3R是一种策略感知的评分标准奖励框架，通过自适应调整评分标准权重，在保持人类权重和类别平衡的同时，利用rollout级别对比来强调当前区分策略输出的标准，从而在更少的训练步数内提升多模态和纯文本任务的奖励质量与严格完成率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于评分标准的奖励（Rubric-based rewards）中，静态聚合方式将标准的人类重要性与其作为优化信号的当前有用性混为一谈，导致许多重要标准已饱和或不可达，而区分rollout的标准未必具有最大人类权重，这降低了强化学习后训练的效率。

Method: 提出POW3R框架：在保持人类权重和类别平衡作为评分标准目标的同时，自适应调整训练过程中评分标准的奖励权重；利用rollout级别对比来强调当前能够区分策略输出的标准，使GRPO奖励更具信息量但不改变底层评估目标。

Result: 在三种基础策略、两个数据集（多模态和纯文本）上，POW3R在30个基础策略/指标对比中获胜24次，同时提高了平均评分标准奖励和严格完成率（响应满足所有评分标准要求的提示比例），并以2.5-4倍更少的训练步数达到相同的稳定水平。

Conclusion: 评分标准奖励应当区分最终答案中应重要的事项与当前可以教导策略的事项，即策略感知的自适应权重调整比静态聚合更有效。

Abstract: Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards has made post-training highly effective when correctness can be checked automatically. However, many important model behaviors require satisfying several qualitative criteria at once. Rubric-based rewards address this setting by grading prompt-specific criteria and aggregating them into a scalar reward. Yet standard static aggregations conflate a criterion's human-assigned importance with its current usefulness as an optimization signal. We show that this assumption breaks down in rubric RL: many important criteria are already saturated or currently unreachable, while criteria that distinguish rollouts are not necessarily those with the largest human weights. We introduce POW3R, a policy-aware rubric reward framework that preserves human weights and category balance as the rubric objective while adapting criterion-level reward weights during training. POW3R uses rollout-level contrast to emphasize criteria that currently separate the policy's outputs, making the GRPO reward more informative without changing the underlying evaluation target. Across three base policies on two datasets spanning multimodal and text-only settings, POW3R wins $24$ of $30$ base-policy/metric comparisons, improving both mean rubric reward and strict completion (the fraction of prompts whose response satisfies every required rubric criterion) over vanilla GRPO with rubric rewards, and reaches the same plateau in $2.5$--$4\times$ fewer training steps. Rubric rewards should therefore distinguish what should matter in the final answer from what can teach the current policy.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前生产级LLM Agent将随机模型输出与确定性软件系统结合，但二者之间的边界未被作为一等架构对象来对待，缺乏系统化的设计原语和模式分类。

Method: 定义SDB为四部分契约（提议者、验证者、提交步骤、拒绝信号），围绕它组织协调/状态/控制三个关注点，提出六个运行时模式，并给出五步模式选择方法论和故障诊断流程。

Result: 提出了SDB原语、六个运行时模式（层级委派、散布-聚合+Saga、事件驱动序列、共享状态机、监督者+门控、人在回路）、五步选择方法论、回放发散故障模式，以及将每次调用的模型方差与架构动量分离的可靠性分解。

Conclusion: 随着模型方差降低，模式选择和SDB强度将成为长期可靠性的重要杠杆；方法论应用于五个工作负载，并提供了一个90天合同续约Agent的可运行参考实现。

Abstract: Production LLM agents combine stochastic model outputs with deterministic software systems, yet the boundary between the two is rarely treated as a first-class architectural object. This paper names that boundary the stochastic-deterministic boundary (SDB): a four-part contract among a proposer, verifier, commit step, and reject signal that specifies how an LLM output becomes a system action. We argue that the SDB is the load-bearing primitive of production agent runtimes.
  Around this primitive, we organize agent runtime design into three concerns: Coordination, State, and Control. We present a catalog of six runtime patterns that compose the SDB differently across conversational, autonomous, and long-horizon agents: hierarchical delegation, scatter-gather plus saga, event-driven sequencing, shared state machine, supervisor plus gate, and human in the loop. For each pattern, we trace its lineage to distributed-systems concepts and identify what changes when the worker is stochastic.
  The paper contributes a five-step methodology for selecting runtime patterns, a diagnostic procedure that maps production failures to pattern weaknesses, and a failure mode called replay divergence, in which LLM-based consumers of a deterministic event log produce different downstream outputs under model-version or prompt changes. A stylized reliability decomposition separates per-call model variance from architectural momentum, motivating the claim that as model variance decreases, pattern choice and SDB strength become increasingly important levers for long-run reliability. We apply the methodology to five workloads and provide one runnable reference implementation for a 90-day contract-renewal agent.

### [219] [IterSIMP-σ: Evaluating LLM-Assisted Spatial Interventions in Stress-Aware Topology Optimization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19110)
*Shaoliang Yang,Jun Wang,Yunsheng Wang*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出IterSIMP-σ框架，将多模态大语言模型(LLM)作为可检视的空间提议模块，嵌入应力感知拓扑优化流程。实验表明该框架具备可检视性和可行性，但LLM视觉推理尚未显著提升应力约束优化性能。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多模态大语言模型能否作为可检视的空间提议模块，用于应力感知拓扑优化，以增强设计自动化流程的可解释性和可干预性。

Conclusion: IterSIMP-σ可作为可检视的LLM辅助设计自动化框架，但目前尚无证据表明LLM视觉推理能显著改善应力约束优化性能。

Abstract: This paper studies whether multimodal large language models (LLMs) can serve as inspectable spatial proposal modules for stress-aware topology optimization. IterSIMP-σ keeps the SIMP optimizer as a compliance-minimizing finite-element solver and places a deterministic stress pass, gate evaluator, and hybrid LLM/rule interpreter around it. After each solve, density and von Mises stress fields are rendered; the interpreter proposes ranked spatial interventions; and deterministic safeguards accept, reject, or stop each action. The main action is a soft density seed, where selected elements are initialized at elevated density before the next solve but remain free under the optimality-criteria update. We evaluate the loop on a 16-problem 2D controller-policy benchmark, a six-problem exploratory 3D extension, passive-solid and input ablations, stress-threshold sensitivity, and a fixed-volume attribution study comparing LLM proposals with deterministic max-stress hotspot seeding, random stress-region seeding, and rule-based control. The 2D controller-policy benchmark shows a small retained-compliance difference (1.9% lower geometric mean for the soft-seed LLM), but this diagnostic is not statistically significant (W = 33, two-sided p = 0.382) and is not a fixed-volume feasible-final comparison. In the fixed-volume study, the LLM condition completed 44/48 attempted evaluations; 25/44 completed evaluations produced all-gate-passing retained states. Feasible-final scoring against rule-based control is split 4/4/1, and deterministic exact-hotspot seeding remains competitive. Accepted LLM spatial actions with per-step records have mean normalized seed-to-hotspot distance 0.221. The results support IterSIMP-σ as an inspectable LLM-assisted design-automation framework for spatial interventions, not yet as evidence that LLM visual reasoning improves stress-constrained optimization.

### [220] [Robust Restless Multi-Armed Bandit for Data Center Flexibility Services Through Virtual Machine Scheduling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19116)
*Yifu Ding,Zixi Chen,Thomas Magnanti*

Main category: cs.CE

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于混杂多臂赌博机（RMAB）的框架，用于数据中心需求响应，通过Whittle索引策略和混合算法（结合全局UCB与信任指数）在不确定环境下实现负载削减，并在真实数据集上验证了算法的鲁棒性和优越性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据中心能耗激增给电网带来巨大压力，而需求响应（负载削减）是平衡电网供需的关键手段。然而，实时调度存在资源利用波动、服务质量（QoS）损失不透明等问题，亟需一种无需访问详细调度过程即可实现负载削减的高效框架。

Method: 将每个数据中心的作业到达和重调度建模为马尔可夫决策过程（MDP）中的“不安定臂”，利用开源VM数据集学习状态转移函数；基于Thompson采样推导Whittle索引策略；针对状态空间扩大导致学习变慢的问题，提出混合策略——将全局上置信界（UCB）与信任指数编码相结合，以增强鲁棒性并加速学习。

Result: 所提出的混合策略算法在不同状态空间大小下均保持鲁棒性，持续优于纯Thompson-Whittle（TW）算法（尤其在上下文信息含噪声时），且性能超过当前最优的EXP4框架。

Conclusion: 该RMAB框架能有效实现数据中心需求响应，混合策略有效克服了传统方法的局限性，为电网运营商提供了一种无需内部调度细节即可实现负载削减的可行方案，且代码已开源以支持复现。

Abstract: Energy demands from data centers have surged and stressed the grid in recent years. Electric grids require balancing supply and demand every second, motivating demand response (reduction) from large loads, including data centers. This can be achieved by rescheduling jobs on physical machines. Its real-time implementation is uncertain due to fluctuating resource utilization, and rescheduling incurs quality-of-service (QoS) losses that providers are unwilling to disclose. We propose a restless multi-arm bandit (RMAB) framework in which the grid operator requests load reductions without access to detailed job-rescheduling procedures. Using the open-source virtual machine (VM) datasets, we model job arrivals and rescheduling at each data center as a restless arm in a Markov decision process (MDP), and derive Whittle-index-based policies based on the learned transition function via Thompson sampling. To overcome the weakness of an increasingly long learning process due to an enlarged state space, we used a mixed strategy that included a global upper confidence bound (UCB) encoded with trust indices to enhance robustness and accelerate learning. Results show that the proposed mixed-strategy algorithm remains robust across varying state-space sizes and consistently outperforms the pure Thompson-Whittle (TW) algorithm, especially when contextual information is noisy. It also demonstrates superior performance compared to the state-of-the-art EXP4 framework. We provided an open-sourced code for reproducibility.

*Hyoungsung Kim,Yong-Suk Park*

Abstract: Automated Market Makers face a geometric dilemma: expanding liquidity depth to reduce execution slippage increases Liquidity Providers' exposure to toxic arbitrage, quantified as Loss-Versus-Rebalancing (LVR). We study the Hybrid Liquidity-Collateral Pool (HLCP), a stylized architecture that aims to partially decouple execution quality from active risk exposure through an N-scaled virtual invariant and a collateral buffer. The analysis first characterizes the geometric divergence between execution slippage and marginal-price deviation, then uses this divergence to motivate a trigger-based collateral injection rule. In a stylized duopoly model, under hyper-saturated background liquidity and non-zero volatility or collateral yield, adopting the HLCP is a Nash equilibrium and Pareto-improving relative to a standard AMM benchmark. Empirically, we examine two settings. Under a stochastic-volatility-with-jumps stress scenario, the trigger policy avoids one-shot total buffer depletion under the imposed control law and simulated shock path. Using 2025 Uniswap V2 data with zero collateral yield, the HLCP exhibits lower realized LVR and higher net LP return than the standard CPMM benchmark in the sample considered.

To enable supervised training, we develop a pipeline that extracts latent process motifs from noisy, unstructured legacy topologies and synthesizes high-quality rationale-based Chain-of-Thought (CoT) training data. ### [223] [The fitness landscape of social norms in social dilemmas](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.18834)
*Maximilian Puelma Touzel*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种在社会困境中通过随机信号协调多智能体行为的规范理论，将Morsky & Akçay (2019)的规范分类与理性准则从矩阵博弈扩展至更一般的马尔可夫博弈框架，并给出了复制子动力学的通用解与分析方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 社会规范是解决社会困境（social dilemmas）中多智能体协调问题的重要手段。现有规范理论多基于矩阵博弈，而强化学习领域更常用的马尔可夫博弈框架尚未被充分纳入规范演化分析，亟需一种更一般的理论来统一描述规范在随机环境中的演化与涌现机制。

Method: 将Morsky & Akçay (2019)基于理性准则的规范分类理论从矩阵博弈推广到马尔可夫博弈（Markov game）设定；在信号与奖励空间上对规范进行映射；利用复制子动力学（replicator dynamics）分析规范的演化过程，并给出通用解。

Result: 建立了马尔可夫博弈框架下的规范演化理论，阐明了信号相关性、协调收益与剥削不确定性之间的权衡；给出了复制子动力学的通用解析解法，为规范的涌现提供了理论依据。

Conclusion: 该理论为理解多智能体系统中社会规范的演化提供了更一般的框架，弥合了演化博弈论与强化学习之间的鸿沟，有望为设计去中心化、可广泛采纳的协调机制提供理论指导。

Abstract: By specifying behaviour across multiple agents, social norms are a coordination approach to resolving social dilemmas. Decentralized and wide adoption can be achieved by norms whose prescription involves interpreting stochastic signals in the environment. Such signals must have enough correlation to orchestrate mutually beneficial coordination and enough disincentivizing uncertainty about the benefits of exploiting that coordination. Evolutionary game theory of matrix games has been used to describe how, by rational agents comparing and adopting norms, a norm can evolve to become dominant in a population. Morsky \& Akçay (2019) classify norms according to a set of rationality criteria. Joint player strategies that adopt norms that are consistent with optimal single-player strategies with respect to expected reward naturally satisfy a correlated, rather than Nash game theoretic equilibrium condition. Here, we present a version of this theory that clarifies the basic ingredients. We formulate it in the more general Markov game setting more commonly used in reinforcement learning theory. We illustrate the theory by mapping norms over the signal and reward space, while also giving a detailed exposition of the underlying mechanics of the approach. Finally, we give a general solution and analysis of replicator dynamics, which Morsky \& Akçay (2019) propose as a means by which these norms could emerge.

### [224] [Nash Welfare in Additively Separable Hedonic Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19030)
*Marta Pagano,Alexander Schlenga*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文首次在可加可分享乐博弈（ASHGs）中研究纳什福利最大化，证明了高纳什福利分区满足合理论稳定性等理想性质，并针对不同子类提出了近似算法（AEGs的n-1近似、AFGs的2n近似），同时证明了NP-hard不可近似性以及联盟规模/数量约束下的复杂度边界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASHGs中社会福利最大化的研究长期聚焦于功利主义福利，而纳什福利——一种兼具公平与效率且具有尺度不变性的经济学重要指标——被完全忽视。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用基于打包（packing-based）的近似算法设计，结合不可近似性归约证明；对联盟规模或数量有约束的情形，通过多项式时间算法与NP-hardness归约刻画复杂度边界。

Result: 高纳什福利分区在对称博弈中保证契约纳什稳定性；AEGs子类可近似比为n-1，AFGs子类为2n；一般ASHGs不可近似因子下界为1.0000759；联盟规模或数量有上界2时多项式时间可解，上界3及以上则NP-hard或不可近似。

Conclusion: 纳什福利在ASHGs中具有良好性质但计算困难，本文系统刻画了其近似算法与复杂度边界，为该方向后续研究奠定基础。

Abstract: Additively separable hedonic games (ASHGs) are a prominent model of coalition formation where agents' preferences are derived from their individual valuations of peers. While social welfare maximization in ASHGs has traditionally focused mostly on utilitarian welfare, Nash welfare -- a well-established metric in economics which balances fairness with efficiency and offers scale invariance -- has been entirely overlooked. In this paper, we initiate the study of Nash welfare in ASHGs. We point out desirable properties fulfilled by partitions with high Nash welfare. This includes guaranteed contractual Nash stability in symmetric games, even for any approximation of Nash welfare. This is particularly appealing since, as for other welfare notions, Nash welfare turns out to be NP-hard to maximize, even for the ASHG subclass of symmetric aversion to enemies games (AEGs). A main focus of our study is on approximation algorithms for the Nash welfare objective. We present packing-based algorithms with approximation ratios for well-established subclasses of ASHGs: $n-1$ for AEGs and $2n$ for appreciation of friends games. This is complemented by a strict inapproximability result showing it is NP-hard to approximate Nash welfare within a factor of $1.0000759$ in general ASHGs. Further, we investigate the restricted settings with an upper bound on the coalition size or number of coalitions, and draw the boundary between the cases admitting efficient algorithms and those yielding NP-hardness: bounding the allowed size or number of coalitions by $2$ admits polynomial-time solvability, whereas bounds of $3$ or more yield NP-hardness or unbounded inapproximability.

</details>


### [225] [Distributionally Robust Games via Coherent Risk Measures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19302)
*Bharat Gangwani,Arunesh Sinha*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文研究了数据驱动博弈中玩家面临有限样本推断的收益分布不确定性时的策略互动，提出了以一致效用（风险）度量（包括均值-半偏差和条件风险价值）为核心的分布鲁棒博弈框架，证明了均衡存在性、PPAD完全性等理论结果，并通过数值实验验证了鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据驱动环境下，玩家只能从有限样本中推断收益分布，面临不确定性。现有博弈模型未充分考虑玩家对这类不确定性的校准态度，缺乏将风险敏感性作为偏好原始特征的理论框架。

Method: 采用分布鲁棒博弈框架，以一致效用度量（均值-半偏差、条件风险价值等）建模风险敏感偏好，利用分布鲁棒均衡存在性先验结果证明数据驱动环境下多种模糊集的均衡存在性，分析均衡连续结构，进行PPAD计算复杂性归约，构建多重线性互补规划公式，并开展数值实验。

Result: (1)证明了数据驱动环境下多种模糊集的均衡存在性；(2)揭示了此类博弈本质为连续博弈而非有限矩阵博弈；(3)给出了风险厌恶玩家期望效用损失的上界；(4)证明了PPAD完全性及若干一致效用度量博弈的PPAD成员性；(5)提出了多重线性互补规划公式；(6)数值实验验证了求解的鲁棒性和样本外表现。

Conclusion: 该框架统一了风险理论建模与均衡分析，为数据驱动环境下的风险感知策略决策提供了理论基础，表明风险敏感性是均衡分析中不可忽视的原始特征。

Abstract: We study strategic interaction in data-driven games where players face uncertainty about payoff distributions inferred from finite samples. To model calibrated attitudes toward such uncertainty, we formulate distributionally robust games with a special focus on coherent utility (risk) measures, including Mean-semideviation and Conditional Value-at-Risk. This framework treats risk sensitivity as a primitive feature of player preferences while retaining a formal connection to distributional robustness. We make a number of contributions that are enumerated next. (1) We use prior results for the existence of distributionally robust equilibria to show the existence of equilibria in data-driven settings for various ambiguity sets, and (2) show that these games are inherently continuous, rather than finite matrix games, which fundamentally alters equilibrium structure and precludes direct extensions of standard correlated equilibrium notions. (3) We bound the loss in expected utility that a player can expect from being risk-averse. (4) We further characterize the computational complexity of equilibrium computation, proving PPAD-completeness in general and PPAD membership for several coherent utility measure games. (5) We present multilinear complementarity program formulations for several coherent utility measure games. (6) Numerical experiments reveal the robustness and out of sample performance of the game solutions. Our results unify risk-theoretic modeling and equilibrium analysis, providing a principled foundation for risk-aware strategic decision-making in data-driven environments.

</details>


### [226] [The Privacy Subsidy in Glosten-Milgrom: Bid-Ask Spread and Welfare under Flip-Noise Direction Observation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.19742)
*Yuki Nakamura*

Main category: cs.GT

TL;DR: 本文在Glosten-Milgrom (1985)序贯交易模型中，引入二进制翻转信道(概率η)作为交易方向信号的隐私机制，推导出均衡买卖价差的闭式解为μ(1-2η)Δ，并揭示了每笔交易中存在μηΔ的"隐私补贴"从流动性池向交易者的转移。该结果将隐私补贴概念从连续高斯(Kyle模型)扩展到离散二值微观结构模型，主要应用于基于MPC的ε-差分隐私方向披露的匹配引擎。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将隐私机制(差分隐私)与经典市场微观结构模型(GM模型)相结合，建立信息论视角下隐私对市场质量(价差)和福利影响的严格理论分析。

Method: 在GM序贯交易模型中，将市场做市商对交易方向的观测建模为二进制翻转信道(概率η)，在贝叶斯做市商定价规则下求解均衡价差和福利分解。

Result: 均衡价差为μ(1-2η)Δ；福利分解显示每笔交易存在μηΔ的隐私补贴，即从流动性池向交易者的转移支付。

Conclusion: 隐私补贴概念在离散二值微观结构(GM模型)与连续高斯(Kyle模型)中均成立，具有跨模型的鲁棒性；为MPC等隐私保护交易机制的设计提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We derive a closed-form bid-ask spread and welfare decomposition for the Glosten-Milgrom 1985 sequential-trading model when the market maker observes the trade direction perturbed by a binary flip channel of probability $η$ -- a natural information-theoretic model of privacy mechanisms acting on the direction signal. Under a committed Bayesian market-maker pricing rule, the equilibrium spread is $μ(1-2η)Δ$, where $μ$ is the informed-trader fraction and $Δ= v_H - v_L$ the value range. The welfare decomposition identifies a per-trade transfer $μηΔ$ from the protocol's liquidity pool to traders -- the "privacy subsidy", mirroring the Gaussian-Kyle analog established in prior work. The result extends the privacy-subsidy concept from continuous Gaussian to discrete two-state microstructure, demonstrating robustness across both classical models. Primary application: MPC-based matching engines with $\varepsilon$-differentially-private direction disclosure, where the engine prices on a noisy direction signal.

</details>
